      <meta name="description" content="Join us for a&amp;#160;#CreativeJamPlease join us for a Creative Jam, an inspiring two-part design experience that demonstrates and celebrates creativity.Event will be held in the Student Union,&amp;#160;Ballroom B.&amp;#10;The Adobe Creative Cloud team will host the Creative Jam presentations. This one-hour design showcase highlights the work of 3 local creative leaders. &amp;#10;At the same time, in the next room, student design teams will be competing in the Creative Jam tournament, a 3-hour design charrette showdown. This event will have two categories: motion design and graphic design. Once the Creative Jam presentations wrap, tournament participants will take the stage to share their creations with you. As part of the audience, you&amp;#8217;ll vote on each submission and select the People&amp;#39;s Choice winner. There will also be Grand Prize winners decided by a group of Judges!TOURNAMENT APPLICATIONSubmission form: http://tinyurl.com/creativejamsubmissionDeadline: Sunday, Feb. 19 @ midnightAcceptance sent out: Monday, Feb. 20BEHANCE PORTFOLIO REVIEWSLocal creative leaders will be on site and would love to see your work.The reviews are a 1-on-1 opportunity to meet for 15 minutes with a creative professional before the main event. Getting feedback is valuable in knowing how to attract new clients and represent your work.Sigh up here:&amp;#160;http://tinyurl.com/creativejamreview&amp;#160;and we will provide you with the exact time and place of your review.EVENT SCHEDULE&amp;#10;7:00pmDoors open. Settle in, and meet your fellow creative community. Free soda and food available.The tournament will be in full swing&amp;#8212;pop your head in and see how it&amp;#8217;s developing. Portfolio reviews will be taking place for those who reserved a spot before the event.&amp;#160;&amp;#10;8:00pmCreative Jam Talks begin. Sit back as local creative leaders walk you through their personal creative process.&amp;#10;9:00pmCreative Jam tournament competitors share their solutions, inspired by a theme announced just 3-hours before.&amp;#160;Audience and Judges vote. Awards follow.&amp;#10;9:30pmEveryone socializes and gets to meet the teams.&amp;#10;&amp;#10;

      <meta name="twitter:description" content="Join us for a&amp;#160;#CreativeJamPlease join us for a Creative Jam, an inspiring two-part design experience that demonstrates and celebrates creativity.Event will be held in the Student Union,&amp;#160;Ballroom B.&amp;#10;The Adobe Creative Cloud team will host the Creative Jam presentations. This one-hour design showcase highlights the work of 3 local creative leaders. &amp;#10;At the same time, in the next room, student design teams will be competing in the Creative Jam tournament, a 3-hour design charrette showdown. This event will have two categories: motion design and graphic design. Once the Creative Jam presentations wrap, tournament participants will take the stage to share their creations with you. As part of the audience, you&amp;#8217;ll vote on each submission and select the People&amp;#39;s Choice winner. There will also be Grand Prize winners decided by a group of Judges!TOURNAMENT APPLICATIONSubmission form: http://tinyurl.com/creativejamsubmissionDeadline: Sunday, Feb. 19 @ midnightAcceptance sent out: Monday, Feb. 20BEHANCE PORTFOLIO REVIEWSLocal creative leaders will be on site and would love to see your work.The reviews are a 1-on-1 opportunity to meet for 15 minutes with a creative professional before the main event. Getting feedback is valuable in knowing how to attract new clients and represent your work.Sigh up here:&amp;#160;http://tinyurl.com/creativejamreview&amp;#160;and we will provide you with the exact time and place of your review.EVENT SCHEDULE&amp;#10;7:00pmDoors open. Settle in, and meet your fellow creative community. Free soda and food available.The tournament will be in full swing&amp;#8212;pop your head in and see how it&amp;#8217;s developing. Portfolio reviews will be taking place for those who reserved a spot before the event.&amp;#160;&amp;#10;8:00pmCreative Jam Talks begin. Sit back as local creative leaders walk you through their personal creative process.&amp;#10;9:00pmCreative Jam tournament competitors share their solutions, inspired by a theme announced just 3-hours before.&amp;#160;Audience and Judges vote.
